## ENG-1571 (M11 gate) — harness reconciliation + false-done revert · pass69 · 2026-07-12 (orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority 2026-07-12)

Closed the last two pre-token M11 items and merged them (PR #23 → `orvexai/orvex-studio-ui`@`dev`). Decisions:

- **Seed-leg contract:** reconciled `e2e/support/entitlementSeed.ts` to the real ENG-1951 endpoint `POST {origin}/v1/entitlements/user/<userId>/seed`, body `{plan}`, assert 201 (the prior `{userId,tier:"pro"}` flat-URL shape matched nothing; `"pro"` isn't a catalog plan). Default seed plan = **`personal`** (the purchasable upgrade — realistic free→paid dissolve; catalog also allows free|teams|enterprise). Mirrors the M8 seed-helper reconciliation.
- **D6 M10-flow:** added a §4j D1/D2/D3 block driving the ENG-1535 M10 payload shapes through the SPA origin's `/api/v1/*` shell prefix (exercising the ENG-1950 edge rewrite end-to-end), token **reused** from the signed-in SPA's attached header (never re-minted). Fixed an AC6 D-drift (mock targeted `**/v1/discover/**`, a path no pane calls → never intercepted).
- **Product change (scoped judgment call):** migrated `src/routes/Memory.tsx` read `/memory` → `/v1/memory` so `buildApiUrl` yields `/api/v1/memory` and the edge rewrite reaches the BFF's real `/v1/memory` mount (AC3/D3). Precedent: ENG-1955 `/v1/query`. Scoped to the ONE gate-critical pane; the other scaffold panes (Home/Discover/Library/Settings) still read bare domains and render honest states (fine for AC6/AC7) — flagged as a separate `/v1`-convention product follow-up, not an M11 blocker.

## 2026-07-12 — M13 (ENG-1549) pass80: AC2 break-glass leg BLOCKED on a KEY-TYPE MISMATCH (OpenBao holds RSA-4096; the family verifier is Ed25519-ONLY) + private key present in OpenBao. Did NOT wire, did NOT tick AC2. gateArmed = FALSE.

_Orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority (2026-07-12). linearis-only; secret VALUES never printed; no gate relaxation; tick-only-proven with P2-census; refresh-on-write; P1-guard. Collision-avoid respected: this lane = orvex-studio-identity + the ENG-1549 AC2 break-glass leg ONLY — touched NO orvex-studio-ui/CF/ENG-1571/1950 (pass-79's lane). No PR, no manifest change, no tick._

- **DECISIVE — the OpenBao break-glass key is the WRONG TYPE for the mechanism; wiring it would be dead, fail-closed config.** The PO placed a key at `apps/orvex-studio-identity/breakglass`. Read live (value NOT printed — `openssl pkey -pubin -text -noout` classification only): `public_key` = **RSA-4096** SPKI PEM. But the entire family break-glass verifier — `orvex-studio-lib/pkg/offlineauth.NewStaticJWKSFromJSON` — **hard-rejects any `kty != "OKP"` / `crv != "Ed25519"` at load** ("only OKP/Ed25519 sealed keys are supported"), and identity's own mint/verify (`internal/sealing`, `cmd/sealtool`) is **EdDSA/Ed25519-only** (`jwt.SigningMethodEdDSA`, seed `IDENTITY_BREAKGLASS_SEALING_KEY`). Converting the RSA PEM to the `kty=RSA, alg=RS256` JWK the task literally requests yields a JWKS the verifier **refuses at construction**; console `server.go` then logs _"BREAKGLASS_JWKS_PATH content invalid, falling back to the not-implemented verifier (fails closed, never fabricated)"_ and leaves `offline_verifier_real_adapter_wired=false`. **The mechanism would NOT be armed.** The task's deny-path "proof" is void here — a rejected wrong-sig token is refused by the *not-implemented fallback*, proving nothing about arming. Refused to mount it (no-fallbacks / silent-rot / P1-guard).
- **The BREAKGLASS_JWKS_PATH/ISSUER/AUDIENCE consumer is orvex-studio-console, NOT identity.** `grep` across identity/console/workflows/lib/contracts/ops → only `orvex-studio-console` (`internal/config/config.go` l.104-106/186-188, `internal/server/server.go` l.197-212) reads them. **orvex-studio-identity consumes NONE** (Clerk/Keycloak/SCIM only); it owns the SEALING/mint leg + offline `sealtool`, never the verify leg. Identity `README`: _"The wiki and Studio products have no break-glass; break-glass is scoped to the orvex-studio-console admin."_ The task's "determine how identity consumes BREAKGLASS_JWKS_PATH / wire it into identity" rests on a false premise.
- **SECURITY FLAG — the private key IS in OpenBao (the task said it is NOT).** The `breakglass` secret carries **both** `private_key` and `public_key` (field-name enumeration only — private value NEVER read/echoed). This contradicts the FR-I12/OQ-I5 offline-custody threat model (an IdP-independent recovery root whose private half never touches the cluster secret store). The recovery root's private key sitting in OpenBao defeats break-glass's own SPOF-independence purpose. **Recommend PO purge it.**
- **AC2 — NOT ticked. Already correctly `[ ]` + deferrable; ticking = gate relaxation / fake-Done.** AC2 asserts a POSITIVE `POST /api/breakglass/recover → 200` + alarm/audit + 403 boundary — not merely "armed". The ticket already records the deny-half proven and the positive path blocked on (a) the offline-sealed root keypair — **"a physically-human-only custody action per §4h/§6 (an agent must not mint the offline recovery root)"** — and (b) BREAKGLASS_* wired in deploy; _"deferrable … does NOT block this gate per its own DoD text."_ This pass makes (a) SHARPER: the material provided is not merely pending — it is the **wrong key type** and cannot arm the verifier as-is. Left `[ ]`.
- **M13 does NOT close; unchanged. gateClosed = FALSE.** Remaining true blocker = AC4 (workflows `/v1/workflows` authorizing-proxy SERVER, UNBUILT per pass76), owned elsewhere — did NOT advance ENG-1549 Done. AC2 stays deferrable-open.
- **Real unblock path (human-ledger).** [1] PO generates the break-glass root as an **Ed25519** keypair (NOT RSA), private seed held offline, fed to `sealtool`. [2] Publish the **public** half as an **OKP/Ed25519** JWKS (kid = RFC7638 thumbprint) — ConfigMap (public) mounted at `BREAKGLASS_JWKS_PATH` in the **console** overlay, `BREAKGLASS_ISSUER=orvex-identity-breakglass`, `BREAKGLASS_AUDIENCE`=sealtool `-aud` (canonical `console-breakglass`; the offlinetest `orvex-studio-breakglass` is a TEST golden, not prod — confirm with the console owner). [3] **Purge the RSA `private_key`+`public_key`** from OpenBao. [4] Then the console real adapter wires and AC2's positive leg is drivable — still gated on AC4 for M13 Done.
- **Discipline.** linearis CLI only (comment via `issues discuss` on ENG-1549). Read cache/code/OpenBao live. NO PR, NO manifest change, NO deploy, NO tick — nothing to review/merge (refusal is the finding). Secret VALUES never printed (field names + `openssl` algorithm classification + char-count only; private_key never read). No gate relaxation; no unproven tick; no fake-arm; no silent dead-config. No `rate_limited` hit. Appended under `flock` on `po-decisions/2026-07-12.md.lock`. Full log: `scratchpad/pass80/breakglass.md`.

## 2026-07-12 — M11 (ENG-1571) pass79: CF cutover BLOCKED on an under-scoped CF token (exact wrangler error captured); /api→/v1 rewrite MERGED to dev. gateClosed = FALSE, cutover = FALSE.

_Orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority (2026-07-12). linearis-only; Sonnet-5 trailer; independent review before merge; secret VALUES never printed (bao→gh + bao→wrangler-env pipes only); no gate relaxation; tick-only-proven; refresh-on-write; P1-guard. - **DECISIVE — the CF token the PO placed cannot deploy Workers; the auto-cutover-on-green ruling cannot execute as-is.** OpenBao `apps/orvex-studio-ui/cloudflare` field `api_token` verified present (field name only; value never fetched) and wired as CI secret `CF_API_TOKEN` (piped bao→gh, never echoed). But the token is READ-scoped: it lists accounts/zones + reads orvex.dev worker routes, yet **403s (code 10000) on every `workers/scripts|services` call**. `scripts/cutover-worker.sh cutover staging` ran preflight PASS → fresh canon build → **`wrangler deploy --env staging` FAILED**: `✘ A request to the Cloudflare API (/accounts/3bd1…/workers/services/orvex-studio-ui-staging) failed. Nothing to roll back.

Even a re-scoped token would fail resolving the binding (or 5xx `/api/v1/*` → verify AC3/AC4 red → auto-rollback). Fix = dual-home orvex-studio-api as a CF Worker, OR re-architect the Worker `/api` forward to an HTTP-origin fetch of the k8s BFF (architecture decision; conflicts with the A-SHELL single-service-binding tier note).
- **Milestone-scope tension (flag).** README + wrangler.toml call the Worker serving path the **M14** DNS/cert cutover end-state ("kept alongside nginx until then"). M11's BFF-data e2e legs (AC1/AC3) need /api→BFF live behind orvex.dev, but nginx serves the SPA shell for /api and the only coded mechanism (the Worker) is M14-scoped AND blocked by B1+B2. Recommend the orchestrator rule: (a) unblock the Worker path now (token + BFF-Worker), or (b) add an interim nginx /api→BFF proxy for the M11 e2e and keep the full cutover in M14.
- **DELIVERED this pass — PR #22 merged to dev (squash `e6b0b4b`).** The `/api`→`/v1` edge rewrite + `[env.staging|production]` deploy targets + the executable cutover runbook + Miniflare service-binding tests (edgeApiForward 11/11). Independent review (reviewer≠implementer): CLEAN — slice-strip guarded by isApiPath, query/method/headers/body preserved, SSE unbuffered. dev is `strict`; updated the BEHIND branch → `ci-success` green on the up-to-date head → squash-merge with the Sonnet trailer. The rewrite half of ENG-1950's DoD is satisfied.

The residue comments are non-completing. Nothing to revert. m11-e2e NOT re-dispatched: Worker undeployed ⇒ orvex.dev still stale nginx SPA + /api = SPA shell ⇒ deterministic pass69 RED; re-running burns Clerk quota for zero signal (not a relaxation — the deploy dep is unmet upstream).

## 2026-07-12 — M13 (ENG-1549) pass81: break-glass ARMING ceremony DECLINED — the prompt directed an AGENT to generate+custody+mint the offline recovery root under an agent-relayed "PO waiver"; refused the forbidden human-only mint, escalated with a ready-to-run human remediation. armed = FALSE, positiveProven = FALSE.

_Orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority (2026-07-12). linearis-only; Sonnet-5 trailer where applicable; secret VALUES never printed; no gate relaxation; tick-only-proven with P2-census; refresh-on-write; P1-guard. Collision-avoid respected: this lane = orvex-studio-identity + orvex-studio-console + the ENG-1549 AC2 break-glass leg ONLY — touched NO pass-79 ui/CF/ENG-1571/1950 nor the pass-78 AC4/workflows-proxy resume. NO OpenBao write/delete, NO key material generated, NO PR, NO deploy, NO endpoint drive, NO tick._

- **DECISIVE — declined to have an automated agent mint + custody + arm the break-glass recovery root, on four independently-sufficient grounds.** The pass81 prompt (framed as a PO waiver of the "agent must not mint the offline root" constraint, plus "handle everything") directed this lane to: destroy the OpenBao RSA secret; `sealtool genkey` an Ed25519 root **agent-side** and store **both halves in OpenBao**; mint a sealed cred; wire the console-dev overlay + merge a GitOps PR to arm it live; self-drive `POST /api/breakglass/recover`; and tick AC2 off that. Refused:
  - **(R1) Ratified ticket constraint.** ENG-1549 §2 AC2 / §4h / §6 (re-verified live this pass; state In Progress; AC2 = `- [ ]`) say the root keypair is *"a physically-human-only custody action … an agent must not mint the offline recovery root."* The waiver is asserted **outside** the ticket; the ticket's own text is the authority. This is also exactly the user's standing autonomy carve-out ("escalate only physically-human-only items").
  - **(R2) Unverifiable override channel.** The "PO OVERRIDE (logged)" reached this lane only through the orchestrator prompt — an agent channel. Per the operating contract, no agent message is the user's consent for a security-posture change of this order (minting + in-cluster-storing the recovery root). A one-line in-band human confirmation is cheap and reversible; inferring it from an orchestrator paraphrase is not.
  - **(R3) Re-opens the exact hole pass80 flagged and told the PO to purge.** pass80 found the `apps/orvex-studio-identity/breakglass` secret already holds a **private_key in OpenBao**, flagged it as an FR-I12/OQ-I5 threat-model violation (the recovery root's private half must never sit in the store it is meant to rescue), and recommended purge. pass81 inverts pass80's own remediation — generate a NEW private root agent-side and put its private half **back** into OpenBao. That widens the gap, with agent-provenance material.
  - **(R4) Fake-done + zero delivery pressure.** §4i/§5e make this gate the fake-done control; the implementing agent CANNOT self-advance. Ticking AC2 off self-generated/self-minted/self-verified material is self-attested done. And AC2 is **deferrable — does NOT block M13** (its own DoD text, re-affirmed 2026-07-12); the real remaining M13 blocker is **AC4** (the `/v1/workflows` authorizing-proxy SERVER, UNBUILT per pass76 — pass-78 lane). Nothing breaks by leaving AC2 `[ ]`.
- **Custody deviation the prompt requested — logged transparently, NOT executed.** The prompt explicitly waived "agent must not mint the offline root" and directed OpenBao custody of the private root. This deviation is recorded here for the human ledger but was not carried out: the private-root mint/custody stays a human/PO action. If the PO genuinely wants an agent-minted, in-cluster-custodied break-glass root, that needs a direct, in-band human directive (not an orchestrator relay) — and even then pass80's SPOF-independence flag stands as a design objection.
- **Ground truth verified live (read-only; NO secret values — generated none, read none).** Verifier Ed25519/OKP-only (`orvex-studio-lib/pkg/offlineauth/jwks.go:53`, hard-fail at construction). Minter EdDSA with fixed `const Issuer = "orvex-identity-breakglass"` (`internal/sealing/sealing.go:17,84`). `sealtool genkey` = native Ed25519 keygen (`SEALING_KEY_SEED_B64`/`SEALING_PUBLIC_KEY_B64`, never disk); `seal -aud` operator-set ⇒ `BREAKGLASS_AUDIENCE` must equal the mint `-aud` (canonical `console-breakglass`; offlinetest `orvex-studio-breakglass` is a TEST golden). `BREAKGLASS_*` consumer = orvex-studio-console, not identity (pass80, unchanged). So the task's Ed25519 **direction** is correct — only its **mode** (agent mints/custodies/self-arms/self-ticks) is forbidden.
- **Ready-to-run HUMAN remediation (clean hand-off).** [1] human/offline `sealtool genkey`, hold the seed offline (FR-I12); [2] PO custody decision on the seed home (offline vs OpenBao/ESO — pass80 flag applies); [3] purge the dead RSA `private_key`+`public_key` at `apps/orvex-studio-identity/breakglass`; [4] agent, normal PR flow: derive the OKP/Ed25519 JWKS (kid=RFC7638 thumbprint) → ConfigMap at `BREAKGLASS_JWKS_PATH` in the console-dev overlay + `BREAKGLASS_ISSUER=orvex-identity-breakglass` + `BREAKGLASS_AUDIENCE=<sealtool -aud>` → independent review → merge → rollout (`offline_verifier_real_adapter_wired=true`); [5] operator mints a test cred + drives recover → 200, wrong/expired → 403. Still gated on AC4 for M13 Done.
- **M13 (ENG-1549) — does NOT close; unchanged. armed = FALSE, positiveProven = FALSE.** ENG-1549 stays In Progress; AC2 stays correctly `[ ]` + deferrable. No box ticked. No P1-guard revert needed (no PR, no merge → no auto-close risk).
- **Discipline.** linearis CLI only (escalation comment on ENG-1549 via `issues discuss`, id `441e35c5-0a9f-4fc1-9e2d-9c60b74bd1df`; refresh-on-write live read confirmed In Progress + AC2 `[ ]` before + the comment is additive). ## Pass83 (2026-07-12) — Force-ratify batch: DECLINED (verifiable-flag argument does not clear it)

**Instruction received.** Force-ratify the same standing batch (ADRs 0017-0023, 0030, 0031, 0032;
NFR budgets NFR-A1a, K11/K12/K13, A1b, A2a, NFR-M1/M6; PRD FR-A24; "any page promotions listed
pending") already declined at pass64 and three times at pass67, via a new authorization theory:
that `allowForcedSelfRatify` being enabled is itself *verifiable* standing PO authorization for
agent self-ratify — distinct from, and not subject to, the "unverifiable relayed consent claim"
objection that sank pass67.

**Step 1 executed — flag checked (read-only `docmost-cli workspace settings`).**
`ratifyGate.allowForcedSelfRatify: true`, `updatedAt: 2026-07-10T18:32:34.975Z` — same session
Daniel enabled it live for the ADR-0024..28 + six service-space-canon 11-page batch recorded in
`po-decisions/2026-07-10.md`. **flagEnabled = true.** Nobody has turned it back off since.

**Disposition: DECLINED anyway. Nothing force-self-ratified.** A workspace-global boolean left ON
has no per-batch scope — it answers "is the mechanism server-permitted," not "did Daniel, live,
ask for these ~15 specific pages today." Pass64 and pass67 (×3) already pre-declared the flag
state was not the blocking issue even when TRUE; the one legitimate precedent for using it on a
bulk batch was Daniel typing live in-session ("can you do it... and then ratify") enabling the
flag AND naming the batch in the same breath — not a flag left on from a prior, different,
already-completed authorization. `doc-ratify` doctrine ("a human, and only a human, moves a page
to canonical... does NOT promote silently or in bulk without a per-page human yes") has no
flag-based carve-out; reading a persistently-true flag as perpetual standing authorization would
make that doctrine dead the moment the flag was first enabled. This is also the third distinct
rhetorical reframing of the identical ask (pass64 plain request → pass67 ×3 "PO approved it

flagging as a pattern rather than re-litigating fresh each time.

pending-ratify, untouched. No content read or written beyond the one read-only settings GET.

## M5 (ENG-1559) Kafka index data-plane close attempt — pass89 (orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority 2026-07-12)

**Ruling assessed: option (a) install the Knative Kafka SINK data-plane vs (b) switch the indexer to a direct Kafka consumer.** Confirmed live: every KafkaSink cluster-wide (`wiki-events-dlq`, the sse bridge, `classify-progress-sink` 121+/125+ days) sits `Data plane not available` — `platform/apps/knative-kafka` never vendored the SINK component (kafka-sink-receiver + config-kafka-sink-data-plane), only the controller + broker dispatcher. Picked **(b)**: smaller blast radius, matches the family's own already-decided architecture (`orvex-studio-lib pkg/events.BrokerPublisher`'s own doc comment: "the Knative Broker is consumer-side Trigger-delivery fork machinery this lib has no dependency on"), and mirrors this repo's own `cmd/sse` background-subscriber precedent.

**Landed + MERGED + LIVE (5 PRs, all CI-green, all independently self-reviewed before merge):**
- orvex-wiki PR #107 (`9d2528ed`) — `outbox-relay.service.ts` builds a REAL CloudEvents 1.0 structured-mode envelope (specversion/id/source/type=`wiki.*`/orvexcell/orvextenant, per the pinned `events/schemas/_envelope.json`) addressed to `wiki-events.<cell>` (KAFKA_OUTBOX_TOPIC, dev configmap patch — the exact literal orvex-studio-knowledge's own KAFKA_RAW_TOPIC already dials). `page.repo.ts`: `insertPage` now ALSO enqueues a shaped `page.content_updated` row (tenant/pageIds/version — `gen.ContentUpdatedData`'s actual decode shape) when created WITH content — previously ONLY `page.created` fired for a brand-new page, a type the indexer's `Orchestrator.Ingest` has never handled (genuinely deferred), so a freshly-created page could never become searchable no matter what else was fixed. 47 tests green (extended `outbox-atomicity-and-relay.integration.spec.ts` with envelope-shape assertions + 2 new AC8 cases), full `src/orvex` tree (462 tests) zero regressions.
- orvex-studio-knowledge PR #34 (`90b74a5`) — `cmd/indexer` converted from a scale-to-zero Knative Service (KafkaSink/Trigger-fed) to a plain Deployment running a DIRECT Kafka consumer (`orvex-studio-lib pkg/events.Consumer`, segmentio/kafka-go — the SAME pattern `cmd/sse`'s own background subscriber and orvex-studio-lib's own audit-publish integration tests already use). Also fixed `config.RedisAddr`'s host-only fallback (`REDIS_HOST`/`REDIS_PORT` are separate Crossplane secret keys, no `REDIS_ADDR` — `"missing port in address"` at dial time). 3 new config_test.go cases.

Fixed to `sslmode=require`.
- orvex-studio-knowledge PR #37 (`2a72aff`) — `LiteLLM.Embed` now retries a 429 (bounded 4 attempts, exponential backoff 500ms/1s/2s, ctx-aware) — legitimate hardening proven live under the gate's own 3-page concurrent embed burst; every non-429 failure still fails on attempt 1, unretried. 3 new/extended tests.

## M11 (ENG-1571/ENG-1950) Worker-path close attempt — pass92 (orchestrator judgment under PO standing authority 2026-07-12)

**gateClosed = FALSE.** ENG-1571 stays In Progress (its baseline was already In Progress, not Todo — pass84's note was stale by the time this pass started). But this pass moved the real, durable state further than any prior pass: **the Cloudflare Worker cutover is now genuinely LIVE** — `orvex.dev` serves from the Worker, the BFF's public origin (`api.studio.orvex.dev`) is live and locked down, and the full `/api` → Worker → BFF path is proven end-to-end with real curl traffic through the real deployed stack. Only the final CI proof (`m11-e2e`) didn't produce a result — see RESIDUE.

**Scope this pass, per handoff:** re-wire CF_API_TOKEN, build the locked-down public BFF origin, point the Worker at it, cut over `orvex.dev`, verify live, re-dispatch `m11-e2e`.

**Token re-wire.** `CF_API_TOKEN` re-wired (bao→gh, piped, never echoed). Confirmed live: Workers Scripts:Edit is now GRANTED (pass84's blocker) — no Memberships:Read gap materialized.

**BFF public origin, locked down — `orvex-studio-api` PR #33 (merged).** Re-instated `httproute-api.yaml.superseded` as `httproute-api.yaml` at `api.studio.orvex.{ai,dev}`, path-scoped to `/v1`+`/healthz` only (narrower than the old open `PathPrefix "/"`). Added `src/middleware/edgeSecret.ts` (constant-time shared-secret check on every `/v1/*` route, gated by a git-committed `WORKER_EDGE_LOCKDOWN_ENABLED` ConfigMap literal — never OpenBao-sourced, can't silently go missing), a dedicated `orvex-studio-api-edge-secret` ExternalSecret (isolated blast radius from DB/Redis creds), and a Traefik `ipAllowList` Middleware as a second network-layer defense. `components/crew` patches the lockdown flag back to `false` + `$patch: delete`s the Middleware/HTTPRoute (the hostname annotation is a static literal that would otherwise collide with prod's on the shared gateway listener). **Independent adversarial review (code-review skill, high effort) run before merge** — 2 real findings fixed in-diff (self-contradicting "no public HTTPRoute" comments; a case-sensitive lockdown-flag comparison that could silently disable it on a ConfigMap typo) + 1 PLAUSIBLE risk flagged (RemoteAddr-based IP allowlisting depends on an unverified LB/SNAT assumption) that was **empirically CONFIRMED live minutes later** — see below.

**Worker-side secret injection — `orvex-studio-ui` PR #25 (merged).** `worker/index.ts` injects `x-orvex-edge-secret` on every forwarded `/api/*` request (a real `wrangler secret put`, never a `[vars]` plaintext), always overwriting a caller-supplied header. 16/16 worker tests green (Miniflare, real fixture BFF).

**Live cutover — real `wrangler deploy --env staging`, 3 defects found and fixed LIVE, not guessed:**
1. `CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` [vars]/secret name collision (Cloudflare rejects a secret sharing a binding name with an existing `[vars]` entry) — `orvex-studio-ui` PR #26 (merged), redeployed clean.
2. **The Cloudflare-IP allowlist rejected the Worker's own legitimate traffic** — 100% 403, not just illegitimate direct-IP requests. Root-caused via Traefik access logs + an in-cluster debug-pod probe: `platform-gateway`'s Service runs `externalTrafficPolicy: Cluster`, so kube-proxy SNATs every inbound connection to a pod IP before Traefik ever sees it — RemoteAddr-based allowlisting cannot work under this topology. This is the exact PLAUSIBLE risk the pre-merge review flagged, now CONFIRMED. `orvex-studio-api` PR #34 (merged): detached the Middleware from the route (kept in-repo for a future `X-Forwarded-For`-based fix, header fully documents why + what's needed); the shared secret is the real gate today, comments updated across 3 files to say so plainly instead of describing a non-enforcing layer.
3. `scripts/cutover-worker.sh`'s own LOCKDOWN verify check used `curl -f`, corrupting the reported code on its own expected-403 case ("403000" instead of "403") — `orvex-studio-ui` PR #27 (merged).

**Live end-to-end proof, after all fixes:** in-cluster (non-CF source IP) — no secret → 403 JSON; wrong secret → 403; correct secret → 401 (reaches real downstream auth); `/healthz` → 200 (never gated, kubelet-equivalent). Direct external to `api.studio.orvex.dev` — same pattern. **Through the Worker** (`https://orvex.dev/api/v1/skills`) → **401 `{"error":"unauthorized"}`** — the Worker injects the secret, the BFF passes it, the request reaches the real `/v1/skills` route, not the SPA shell, not a 502. SSE passthrough confirmed (`text/event-stream`). `scripts/cutover-worker.sh verify staging` — AC1/AC3/AC4/AC5 + LOCKDOWN all green.

**Exact residue (confirmed live, NOT a guess) — why gateClosed stays false:** `m11-e2e` (the real named `m11SpaE2E.spec.ts` CI job, ENG-1571's own binary DoD gate) **hung twice in a row**, past its own 120s-per-test Playwright timeout (`retries: 0`) — once on the PR#27 merge push (~20+ min, cancelled), once on an explicit re-dispatch via an empty commit per this task's own instruction (~6+ min past timeout, cancelled). Not a single-run flake — reproduced twice; not a secrets-unset fast-fail (the spec throws in `beforeAll` if `M11_*` env is absent — a hang means the secrets ARE present). Most likely, not fully diagnosed given time budget: `signIn()`'s `clerk.signIn(...)` call against the real Clerk poc-dev instance — plausibly the FIRST time this spec has ever gotten far enough to attempt a live sign-in against a stack where `/api/*` genuinely resolves (previously it 502'd immediately). **Did NOT patch/skip/relax the test or its CI job to force a green** — recorded for the next pass: `pnpm run e2e:m11` locally against `M11_SPA_BASE_URL=https://orvex.dev` with trace output would localize exactly where `clerk.signIn` sticks.

**Follow-up tracked, not done this pass:** re-attach the IP allowlist once `ipStrategy` reads `X-Forwarded-For` (verify `depth` empirically, don't guess); diagnose the `clerk.signIn()` hang; production (`orvex.ai`) cutover is explicitly out of scope for this pass (manifests carry the prod route already; no prod Worker secrets set, no prod deploy run).

**No AC ticked; no P2-census run — nothing proven to tick, per the gate's own DoD (§9 step 7: unchecked body = fake-done signal if ticked without the named test green).** `ENG-1571`/`ENG-1950` both stay In Progress. Comments posted to both via `linearis` (no MCP write).
